<div id="what-is-mean-total-number-of-steps-taken-per-day" class="section level1">
<h1>What is mean total number of steps taken per day?</h1>
<p>1 - Total number of steps per day</p>
<pre class="r"><code>        # select only steps and date columns
        steps_date &lt;- subset(activity, , select = c(&quot;steps&quot;, &quot;date&quot;))        
        sum.steps &lt;- steps_date %&gt;% group_by(date) %&gt;% summarise_each(funs(sum))</code></pre>
<p>2 - Histogram fo the total number of steps taken per day</p>

<pre><code>## [1] 10766.19</code></pre>

<pre><code>## [1] 10765</code></pre>

<div id="what-is-the-average-daily-activity-pattern" class="section level1">
<h1>What is the average daily activity pattern?</h1>
<p>1 . A time serie plot of the 5 minute interval and the average number of steps taken</p>
<pre class="r"><code>        steps_interval &lt;- subset(activity, , select = c(&quot;steps&quot;, &quot;interval&quot;))
        mean.steps &lt;- steps_interval %&gt;% group_by(interval) %&gt;% summarise_each(funs(mean(., na.rm = TRUE)))
        with(mean.steps, plot(mean.steps$steps,type = &quot;l&quot;))</code></pre>

<p>2 . The maximum number of steps</p>
<pre class="r"><code>max(mean.steps$steps)</code></pre>
<pre><code>## [1] 206.1698</code></pre>
</div>
<div id="imputing-missing-values" class="section level1">
<h1>Imputing missing values</h1>
<p>1 . Number of missing values in the dataset</p>
<pre class="r"><code> sum(is.na(activity$steps))</code></pre>
<pre><code>## [1] 2304</code></pre>
<p>2 . Strategy for filling in tha all of the missing values in dataset.<br /> I used the mean for that 5-minute interval</p>
<p>3 . New dataset with the missing data filled in.</p>
<pre class="r"><code>        activity2 &lt;- activity
        merged &lt;- merge(activity2, mean.steps, by = &quot;interval&quot;)
        for ( i in 1:nrow(activity2)) {
                if (is.na(activity2$steps[i]) == TRUE) {
                        activity2$steps[i] = merged$steps.y[i]
                }
        }</code></pre>
<p>4 . Histogram of the total number of steps taken each day</p>
<pre class="r"><code>  steps_date2 &lt;- subset(activity2, , select = c(&quot;steps&quot;, &quot;date&quot;))
        sum.steps2 &lt;- steps_date2 %&gt;% group_by(date) %&gt;% summarise_each(funs(sum))
        
        hist(sum.steps2$steps, main = paste (&quot;Histogram of steps&quot;), xlab = &quot;steps&quot;, ylim = c(0,30))</code></pre>

<div id="are-there-differences-in-activity-patterns-between-weekdays-and-weekends" class="section level1">
<h1>Are there differences in activity patterns between weekdays and weekends?</h1>
<p>1 . New factor indicationg whether is a weekday or a weekend day</p>
<pre class="r"><code>        library(lubridate)
        for ( i in 1:nrow(activity2)) {
                if (wday(ymd(activity$date[i])) == 1 ) {
                        activity2$weekday[i] = &quot;weekend&quot;
                } else
                        if (wday(ymd(activity$date[i])) == 7 ) {
                                activity2$weekday[i] = &quot;weekend&quot; 
                        } else
                                activity2$weekday[i] = &quot;weekday&quot;
        }</code></pre>
<p>2 . Time serie plot</p>
<pre class="r"><code>        library(lattice)
        steps_date3 &lt;- subset(activity2, , select = c(&quot;steps&quot;, &quot;interval&quot;, &quot;weekday&quot;))
        mean.steps3 &lt;- steps_date3 %&gt;% group_by(interval, weekday) %&gt;% summarise_each(funs(mean))
        xyplot(steps ~ interval | weekday, data = mean.steps3, type = &quot;l&quot;)</code></pre>
